## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the population growth rate (dP/dt) as a function of time (t) and current population size (P). This is a classic population dynamics problem where the growth rate depends on population size through various density-dependent and density-independent mechanisms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Exponential (Malthusian) growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Density-independent growth where rate is proportional to population size'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decreasing logarithmically as population approaches carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Allee effect growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Growth with strong Allee effect where small populations decline'}
- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Growth as balance between anabolic (power-law) and catabolic (linear) terms'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Flexible sigmoidal growth model generalizing logistic'}
- {'name': 'Power-law growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Generalized density-dependent growth with fractional scaling'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2', 'scenario': 'Linear per-capita growth rate with quadratic correction'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent logistic', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * exp(c2 * t)', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with time-varying intrinsic growth rate'}
- {'name': 'Harvesting/immigration-modified growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with constant immigration or harvesting term'}
- {'name': 'Polynomial per-capita rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = P * (c0 + c1 * P + c2 * P**2)', 'scenario': 'Cubic population dynamics with higher-order density effects'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent regulation → multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) limiting growth at high population
- Allee effects → additional multiplicative factor (P - c) introducing a minimum viable population threshold
- Proportionality to population → dP/dt should generally contain P as a multiplicative factor since growth requires existing individuals
- Logarithmic saturation → log(c/P) term indicates Gompertz-type diminishing returns near carrying capacity
- Balance of gain and loss → difference of two power-law terms c0*P^a - c1*P^b with b > a represents competing growth and mortality
- Time-explicit modulation → multiplicative time-dependent factors like exp(c*t) or (1+c*t) indicate changing environmental conditions
- Sign change in growth rate → polynomial in P with roots corresponding to equilibria (extinction, carrying capacity, Allee threshold)
- Per-capita rate analysis → dP_dt / P should simplify to a function of P alone for autonomous density-dependent models
